 When we talk about the treatment of cancer, the first important aspect in this is the timely detection of the disease
 diagnosis ke baad treetment aata he jisase judi kai baaten hai
 The penetration of new technology in all these areas has emerged as an effective weapon in fighting this disease
 lekin hamen hameshaa apni sehat ko lekar khud jaagruk rahanaa chahie kyonki samay par beemaari kaa pataa lagane par kharch bhi kam aata he, said effects bhi kam hote hai or sahi hone kii sambhaavnaaen bhi zyada rahati hai
 If we talk about cancer according to gender, then cases of breast cancer, uterine cervix cancer and ovary cancer are more in women, whereas prostate and lung cancer are more common in men
 breast cancer main digital mammography se beemaari ko jaldi pakadaa ja saktaa he
 Apart from this, MRI is also a technology and thermoelastography about breast tumors also works
 ek samay tha jab breast cancer main puri breast ko hi nikaal diya jaataa tha
 If the disease is detected on time, then the need to remove the breast has reduced significantly
 isse mahilaon kaa aatmavishvaas bhi kam nahin hota or esthetic pahalu bhi bana rahata he
 The complete treatment of cancer rests on several levels, including diagnosis, medicine, radiotherapy, and surgery
 surgery ke kshetra main hui nai tarakkee ko samajhane ke liye ham silsilewar dhang se kadam badhaate hai:surgery se pehlepat (pojishan anisan tomography) scanning yah technology sabhi prakaar ke cancer main madadgaar hoti he
 This makes it very easy to detect the disease and its condition
 yah tumor kii ore bakhubi ishaara kar detii he
 What is the treatment going on and how much is benefiting from it, it is also known by the PAT scan
 colposcopy iskaa istemaal servix cancer main hota he
 In this Vajaina and Cervix are visualized and detailed information about cancer attempts is made
 ultrasound or siti scan isse radiation nahin judi he
 If the cancer is in early stage then ultrasound can be used well
 lekin isaki khami yahi he ki yah puri tarah oparator par nirbhar karata he
 Experience matters a lot in this
 ultrasound ke baad siti scan kii baari aati he
 New surgerygama Knives Radiosurgery It is used radiation therapy to treat anomalies and tumors in the brain
 isamen vishesh upkarnon ke madhyam se radiation kii beam sidhe tumor par kii jaati he, ilaaj ekadam sateek hota he or mastishk ke baaki hisse ko bhi nuksaan nahin pahunchataa
 This technique is a bit expensive but very effective
 steriotactic surgery yah surgery thodi mahangi he lekin sharir ke kisi bhi hisse ko kam se kam nuksaan pahunchaakar kii ja sakati he
 It detects small targets inside the body using a three dimensional coordinate system
 phir iske jariye un par bypsy, radiosurgery, injection jaisi prakriyaaon ko anjaam diya jaataa he
 Bracky Therapy Radioactive seeds or sources are placed close to the tumor
 isse tumor vaale hisse ko target kiya jaataa he

 sivi raman ne prakaash prakirnan ke kshetra main avismaraneey yogadan diya
